isOpen: boolean;\\n  onClose: () => void;\\n  onComplete: () => void;\\n  onBack: () => void;\\n}\\n\\ntype Step = 'phone' | 'otp' | 'profile' | 'dashboard' | 'upload' | 'pipeline' | 'complete';\\n\\nconst STEPS: { id: Step; label: string }[] = [\\n  { id: 'phone', label: 'Phone Number' },\\n  { id: 'otp', label: 'Verification' },\\n  { id: 'profile', label: 'Profile' },\\n  { id: 'dashboard', label: 'Dashboard' },\\n  { id: 'upload', label: 'Upload' },\\n  { id: 'pipeline', label: 'Processing' },\\n  { id: 'complete', label: 'Complete' }\\n];\\n\\nconst THEME = { teal: '#004236', gold: '#B8860B', goldLight: '#F5EC9B' };\\n\\nconst VendorFlow: React.FC<VendorFlowProps> = ({ isOpen, onClose, onComplete, onBack }) => {\\n  const [step, setStep] = useState<Step>('phone');\\n  const [vendorData, setVendorData] = useState({\\n    phone: '',\\n    profile: '',\\n    beautifiedProfile: '',\\n    catalogFile: null as File | null\\n  });\\n  \\n  const hasSpokenRef = useRef(false);\\n  const navStack = useNavStack({ id: 'vendor:phone', label: 'Phone Number' });\\n\\n  // Handle voice commands\\n  const handleCommand = useCallback((cmd: string) => {\\n    console.log('\\ud83c\\udfaf VendorFlow command:', cmd, 'step:', step);\\n    \\n    // Global commands\\n    if (cmd.includes('stop') || cmd.includes('quiet')) {\\n      voice.stop();\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    if (cmd.includes('close') || cmd.includes('exit') || cmd.includes('cancel')) {\\n      voice.stop();\\n      onClose();\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    if (cmd.includes('back') || cmd.includes('go back') || cmd.includes('previous')) {\\n      goBack();\\n      return;\\n    }\\n\\n    // Step-specific handling\\n    if (step === 'phone') {\\n      const digits = extractDigits(cmd);\\n      if (digits.length >= 10) {\\n        setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, phone: digits.slice(0, 10) }));\\n        voice.speak(`Got it: ${speakablePhone(digits.slice(0, 10))}. Say \\\"confirm\\\" or click Send OTP.`);\\n        return;\\n      }\\n      if ((cmd.includes('confirm') || cmd.includes('yes') || cmd.includes('send') || cmd.includes('correct')) && vendorData.phone.length >= 10) {\\n        goToStep('otp', 'Verification');\\n        voice.speak(\\\"Sending code now. For demo, enter 1 2 3 4 5 6.\\\");\\n        return;\\n      }\\n    }\\n\\n    if (step === 'otp') {\\n      const digits = extractDigits(cmd);\\n      if (digits.length >= 6 || cmd.includes('123456')) {\\n        voice.speak(\\\"Verified! Let's build your profile.\\\");\\n        setTimeout(() => goToStep('profile', 'Profile'), 1000);\\n        return;\\n      }\\n    }\\n\\n    if (step === 'profile') {\\n      if (cmd.includes('save') || cmd.includes('confirm') || cmd.includes('yes') || cmd.includes('looks good')) {\\n        goToStep('dashboard', 'Dashboard');\\n        voice.speak(\\\"Profile saved! Welcome to your dashboard.\\\");\\n        return;\\n      }\\n    }\\n\\n    if (step === 'dashboard') {\\n      if (cmd.includes('upload') || cmd.includes('catalog') || cmd.includes('go live')) {\\n        goToStep('upload', 'Upload');\\n        voice.speak(\\\"Upload your catalog. PDF, Excel, or CSV.\\\");\\n        return;\\n      }\\n    }\\n\\n    if (step === 'complete') {\\n      if (cmd.includes('view') || cmd.includes('products') || cmd.includes('catalog') || cmd.includes('show')) {\\n        onComplete();\\n        return;\\n      }\\n    }\\n  }, [step, vendorData.phone, onClose, onComplete]);\\n\\n  // Handle digits from voice\\n  const handleDigits = useCallback((digits: string) => {\\n    console.log('\\ud83d\\udcf1 Digits received:', digits, 'step:', step);\\n    \\n    if (step === 'phone' && digits.length >= 3) {\\n      const phone = digits.slice(0, 10);\\n      setVendorData(d => ({ ...d, phone }));\\n      if (digits.length >= 10) {\\n        voice.speak(`${speakablePhone(phone)}. Confirm?`);\\n      }\\n    }\\n    \\n    if (step === 'otp' && digits.length >= 6) {\\n      voice.speak(\\\"Verified!\\\");\\n      setTimeout(() => goToStep('profile', 'Profile'), 1000);\\n    }\\n  }, [step]);\\n\\n  const voice = useVoice({ \\n    onCommand: handleCommand, \\n    onDigits: handleDigits,\\n    autoStart: isOpen,\\n    pauseTimeout: 10000\\n  });\\n\\n  // Handle text input from AgentBar\\n  const handleTextSubmit = useCallback((text: string) => {\\n    console.log('\\ud83d\\udcdd Text submitted:', text, 'step:', step);\\n    \\n    // Check for digits first\\n    const digits = extractDigits(text);\\n    if (digits.length > 0) {\\n      handleDigits(digits);\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Otherwise process as command\\n    handleCommand(text.toLowerCase());\\n  }, [handleDigits, handleCommand, step]);\\n\\n  // Navigation\\n  const goBack = useCallback(() => {\\n    voice.stop();\\n    const stepOrder: Step[] = ['phone', 'otp', 'profile', 'dashboard', 'upload', 'pipeline'];\\n    const idx = stepOrder.indexOf(step);\\n    \\n    if (idx === 0) {\\n      onBack();\\n    } else {\\n      const prev = stepOrder[idx - 1];\\n      setStep(prev);\\n      navStack.pop();\\n      voice.speak(`Going back.`);\\n    }\\n  }, [step, onBack, navStack, voice]);\\n\\n  const goToStep = useCallback((newStep: Step, label: string) => {\\n    navStack.push({ id: `vendor:${newStep}`, label });\\n    setStep(newStep);\\n  }, [navStack]);\\n\\n  // Welcome message\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (isOpen && step === 'phone' && !hasSpokenRef.current) {\\n      hasSpokenRef.current = true;\\n      const timer = setTimeout(() => {\\n        voice.speak(\\\"Welcome! Enter your phone number. Say each digit, or type below.\\\");\\n      }, 500);\\n      return () => clearTimeout(timer);\\n    }\\n  }, [isOpen, step]);\\n\\n  // Cleanup\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (!isOpen) {\\n      voice.stop();\\n      hasSpokenRef.current = false;\\n    }\\n  }, [isOpen]);\\n\\n  if (!isOpen) return null;\\n\\n  const stepIndex = STEPS.findIndex(s => s.id === step);\\n  const stepLabel = STEPS[stepIndex]?.label || step;\\n\\n  return (\\n    <div style={{ \\n      position: 'fixed', \\n      inset: 0, \\n      background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.92)', \\n      zIndex: 10000, \\n      display: 'flex', \\n      justifyContent: 'center', \\n      alignItems: 'center', \\n      padding: '20px' \\n    }}>\\n      <div style={{ \\n        background: `linear-gradient(135deg, ${THEME.teal}, #001a15)`, \\n        borderRadius: '20px', \\n        width: '100%', \\n        maxWidth: '850px', \\n        maxHeight: '92vh', \\n        overflow: 'hidden', \\n        border: `2px solid ${THEME.gold}40`, \\n        display: 'flex', \\n        flexDirection: 'column',\\n        boxShadow: '0 20px 60px rgba(0,0,0,0.5)'\\n      }}>\\n        \\n        {/* Header */}\\n        <div style={{ \\n          padding: '14px 20px', \\n          background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',\\n          borderBottom: `1px solid ${THEME.gold}30`, \\n          display: 'flex', \\n          justifyContent: 'space-between', \\n          alignItems: 'center',\\n          flexShrink: 0\\n        }}>\\n          <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '14px' }}>\\n            <span style={{ fontSize: '1.6em' }}>\\ud83d\\udce6</span>\\n            <div>\\n              <h2 style={{ color: '#fff', margin: 0, fontSize: '1.1em' }}>Vendor Setup</h2>\\n              <span style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '0.8em' }}>Step {stepIndex + 1} of {STEPS.length - 1}</span>\\n            </div>\\n          </div>\\n        </div>\\n\\n        {/* Progress */}\\n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', padding: '10px 20px', gap: '5px', background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)', flexShrink: 0 }}>\\n          {STEPS.slice(0, -1).map((s, i) => (\\n            <div key={s.id} style={{ \\n              flex: 1, \\n              height: '4px', \\n              borderRadius: '2px', \\n              background: stepIndex >= i ?
